---
about_this_resource_text: '<p><strong>Description: </strong>Cosmology continued.  We
  tie the properties of this spacetime to quantities which can be measured, in particular
  the redshift of light which is emitted early in the universe&rsquo;s history but
  is measured now, and three different notions of distance between events and observers.  The
  current standard paradigm for the nature of the universe, and some outstanding problems
  which are the focus of modern research.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Prof.
  Scott Hughes</p>'
course_id: 8-962-general-relativity-spring-2020

  <span m="222630">this</span> <span m="222840">kappa</span> <span m="223220">term.</span>
  <span m="223580">OK.</span> <span m="224100">And</span> <span m="224670">as</span>
  <span m="224790">we</span> <span m="224880">saw</span> <span m="225150">last</span>

  <span m="2444170">parameter</span> <span m="2445910">times</span> <span m="2446210">dp.</span>
  <span m="2448860">Recall</span> <span m="2449250">that</span> <span m="2449370">the</span>
  <span m="2449460">Hubble</span> <span m="2449670">parameter</span> <span m="2452340">is</span>
  <span m="2452670">a</span> <span m="2452850">dot</span> <span m="2453090">over</span>
  <span m="2453360">a, and</span> <span m="2453670">if</span> <span m="2453780">I'm</span>
  <span m="2453870">doing</span> <span m="2454050">this</span> <span m="2454200">right</span>
  <span m="2454410">now,</span> <span m="2454650">that's</span> <span m="2454830">the</span>
  <span m="2455130">value</span> <span m="2455440">of</span> <span m="2455490">the</span>
  <span m="2455580">Hubble</span> <span m="2455730">parameter</span> <span m="2457910">now.</span>
  <span m="2459680">So</span> <span m="2459860">this</span> <span m="2460130">is</span>
  <span m="2460400">the</span> <span m="2460490">Hubble</span> <span m="2460760">Expansion</span>
  <span m="2461045">Law,</span> <span m="2461420">the</span> <span m="2461510">very</span>
  <span m="2461690">famous</span> <span m="2462020">Hubble</span> <span m="2462230">Expansion</span>
  <span m="2462720">Law.</span></p><p><span m="2463880">So</span> <span m="2464030">we</span>

  <span m="2800320">little</span> <span m="2800440">bit</span> <span m="2800560">of</span>

  <span m="4427590">mass,</span> <span m="4428040">the</span> <span m="4428130">Chandrasekhar</span>

  <span m="4429750">one</span> <span m="4429870">of</span> <span m="4429930">my</span>

  <span m="4441600">of</span> <span m="4441660">matter</span> <span m="4441900">participating.</span>
  <span m="4443040">This</span> <span m="4443490">is</span> <span m="4443910">a</span>
